Doesn‚Äôt the hotel understand how to improve? I just want to collect money but don't want to serve.
5. The hotel claims to be on the side of the Qinhuai River, but everyone knows that the Qinhuai River is very long, and only this section has the best scenery. The Qinhuai River on which the hotel is located is pitch black and you can‚Äôt see anything, and the road is closed during holidays. It leads to traffic congestion and makes traveling very inconvenient.
Finally, I would like to advise everyone not to book this hotel, whether they have money or not, and choose a star-rated hotel instead.
